							if(faqD[i].className=="seclev") {
								faqD[i].style.display = "none";
							}

</div><script>
function slideItLeft()
{
var slidingDiv = document.getElementById("slidewrap-in");
var stopPosition = -744;
if (parseInt(slidingDiv.style.left) > stopPosition )
{
slidingDiv.style.left = parseInt(slidingDiv.style.left) + -12 + "px";
setTimeout(slideItLeft, 1);
}
document.getElementById("slileft").style.display = "block";
document.getElementById("sliright").style.display = "none";
}
function slideItRight()
{
var slidingDiv = document.getElementById("slidewrap-in");
var stopPosition = 0;
if (parseInt(slidingDiv.style.left) < stopPosition )
{
slidingDiv.style.left = parseInt(slidingDiv.style.left) + 12 + "px";
setTimeout(slideItRight, 1);
}
document.getElementById("sliright").style.display = "block";
document.getElementById("slileft").style.display = "none";
}
</script>
